      WHEREAS,  the   Suffolk  County  Department  of  Civil  Service  had  certified 
provisional  approval  as  no  active  list  exists  and the  position  was  duly  posted  as  job 
posting #42 of 2024; and  
       
      WHEREAS,  a  current  employee  Kevin  Okula,  in  the  position  of  Wastewater 
Treatment  Plant  Operator  2A  has  applied  for  the  position,  and  meets  all  minimum 
qualifications  per  the Suffolk  County  Department  of  Civil  Service  and  his  department 
head  is  willing  to  promote  him  to  the  position  of  Senior  Wastewater  Treatment  Plant 
Operator 2A.   
       
      NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, this Town Board hereby provisionally 
appoints Kevin OKula to the position of Senior Wastewater Treatment Plant Operator 
2A effective January 1, 2025 and sets his salary at a rate of pay as found on Group 16, 
Step 5A of the CSEA Operational and Technical Salary Schedule which is $67,049.14 
per annum. 
       
RESOLVED, a copy of this resolution be forwarded to payroll, and all Town Hall 
Departments may review and obtain a copy of this resolution from the electronic storage 
device and if needed, a certified copy of same may be obtained from the Office of the 
Town Clerk. 
 
                                  THE VOTE 
                                        
      RESULT:      ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
      MOVER:       Robert Kern, Councilman 
      SECONDER:    Denise Merrifield, Councilwoman 
      AYES:        Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

                            TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
                                        
                            TB Resolution 2025-86 
                                        
    RESOLUTION SETTING FEES FOR TAXICABS AND VEHICLES FOR HIRE 
        PURSUANT TO CHAPTER 281 OF THE RIVERHEAD TOWN CODE 
                                        
             Councilwoman Merrifield offered the following resolution, 
                  which was seconded by Councilwoman Waski 
 
      WHEREAS, the Town Board adopted Chapter 281 of the Riverhead Town Code 
entitled “Taxicabs and Vehicles for Hire” on May 3, 2011 by Local Law No. 16-2011, 
and  
 
      WHEREAS, Section 281-24 of the Riverhead Town Code states that the Town 
Board shall set all fees under chapter 281 by resolution, 
 
      NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, effective January 7, 
2024, the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead, hereby established the following fee 
schedule pursuant to Chapter 281 of the Riverhead Town Code: 
Fee for an owner's license:                           $750.00 
Fee for a vehicle permit:                             $150.00 per vehicle 
Fee for an operator's permit:                         $150.00 
Fee for an appeal of a disapproval,  
suspension hearing or revocation hearing:             $100.00 
 
Late fee:                                             $50.00 
 
Renewal fees: 
       
            Owner's license:                          $250.00 
 
            Vehicle permit:                           $100.00 
             
            Operator's permit:                        $100.00 
 
                                  THE VOTE 
                                        
      RESULT:      ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
      MOVER:       Denise Merrifield, Councilwoman 
      SECONDER:    Joann Waski, Councilwoman 
      AYES:        Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

                            TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
                                        
                            TB Resolution 2025-88 
                                        
RATIFIES AUTHORIZATION FOR THE TOWN ATTORNEY'S OFFICE TO EXECUTE 
SETTLEMENT OF LEGAL ACTION AGAINST ISLAND WATER PARK CORP., D/B/A 
                              SCOTT’S POINTE 
                                        
               Councilwoman Waski offered the following resolution, 
                  which was seconded by Councilman Rothwell 
 
      WHEREAS, a legal action was commenced in the name of the Town of Riverhead 
against Island Water Park Corp. d/b/a Scott’s Pointe, the owner of the property known 
and designated as 5835 Middle Country Road, Calverton, New York, in the Supreme 
Court of the State of New York, County of Suffolk under Index Number: 61646/2024, to 
enjoin the use and occupancy of said property and/or certain portions thereof and all 
penalties in connection with certain violations of the Riverhead Town Code; and 

      WHEREAS, the parties have reached a settlement of that legal action inclusive of all 
costs, expenses and interest; and 

      WHEREAS, in light of the costs attendant to proceeding to a trial together with the 
uncertainties of litigation, the Town Attorney’s Office demanded, and received, certain terms 
of settlement, including civil penalties payable to the Town in the sum of $50,000.00. 

      NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED, that the Town Board of the Town of 
Riverhead be and hereby accepts the settlement reached regarding legal action in the 
name of the Town of Riverhead against Island Water Park Corp. d/b/a Scott’s Pointe, 
the owners 5835 Middle Country Road, Calverton, New York, in the Supreme Court of 
the State of New York, County of Suffolk under Index Number: 61646/2024; and be it 
further,  
 
      RESOLVED, that the Town Board hereby ratifies authorization for the Office of the 
Town Attorney to enter into a stipulation of settlement on behalf of the Town as well as any 
other documents necessary to effectuate the settlement of the litigation; and it is further; 
and be it further, 
 
      RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby directed to forward a certified copy of 
this resolution to the Accounting Department and the Office of the Town Attorney; and be it 
further,  
      
     RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of this 
resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of same 
may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
                                  THE VOTE

NAYS:        Denise Merrifield

                            TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
                                        
                           TB Resolution 2024-1009 
                                        
      SCHEDULES PUBLIC HEARING FOR THE SITE PLAN AMENDMENT 
    APPLICATION OF ISLAND WATER PARK 5835 MIDDLE COUNTRY ROAD, 
                  CALVERTON, NY SCTM NO. 600-135-1-7.34 
                                        
               Councilwoman Waski offered the following resolution, 
                  which was seconded by Councilman Rothwell 
 
      WHEREAS,   the  Riverhead  Town  Board  is  in  receipt  of  a  site  plan  application 
seeking to amend the previously approved site plan of Island Water Park (d/b/a Scott’s 
Pointe); and  
       
      WHEREAS,   the  proposed amendments  include  legalization  of  a  go-kart  track, 
pickleball  courts,  and  conversion  of  an  existing  interior  storage  space  for  use  as  a 
catering/event space; and  
       
      RESOLVED,  that  in  accordance  with  Riverhead  Town  Code  §301-305B(6)(b), 
the Town Clerk is hereby authorized to publish the attached notice of public hearing in 
the the Riverhead News-Review; and be it further 
       
      RESOLVED,   that  in  accordance  with  Riverhead  Town  Code  §301-305B(6)(c), 
the applicant is hereby directed to post the property with the notice of the public hearing 
a minimum of ten days in advance of the public hearing, with notice posted no later than 
January 12th, 2025; and be it further 
       
      RESOLVED,  that  in  accordance  with  Riverhead  Town  Code  §301-305B(6)(d),  
the applicant is hereby directed to forward a certified copy of the public hearing notice 
by certified mail to all property owners within a 200-foot radius of the subject property at 
least ten days prior to the date of the public hearing, with notice postmarked no later 
than January 12th, 2025; and be it further  
       
      RESOLVED¸ that the Town Clerk is hereby authorized to forward a copy of this 
resolution  to Ken  Myers (ken@scottspointe.com),  the  Planning  Department;  the  Town 
Attorney’s office; and be it further 
 
      RESOLVED,  that  all  Town  Hall  Departments  may  review and  obtain  a  copy  of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and if needed, a certified copy of same 
may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk
